```
[132]: FIRST( AddExp '+' MultiExp ) = { '-' '!' '(' '+' '~' 'defined' 'identifier' 'number' }
[133]: FIRST( AddExp '-' MultiExp ) = { '-' '!' '(' '+' '~' 'defined' 'identifier' 'number' }
[134]: FIRST( MultiExp '*' UnaryExp ) = { '-' '!' '(' '+' '~' 'defined' 'identifier' 'number' }
[135]: FIRST( MultiExp '/' UnaryExp ) = { '-' '!' '(' '+' '~' 'defined' 'identifier' 'number' }
[136]: FIRST( MultiExp '%' UnaryExp ) = { '-' '!' '(' '+' '~' 'defined' 'identifier' 'number' }
[137]: FIRST( UnaryOp UnaryExp ) = { '-' '!' '+' '~' 'defined' }
[138]: FIRST( '(' ConstExp ')' ) = { '(' }

```

```Mermaid
syntaxState161 x==x |"'-' '!=' ')' ...

syntaxState162 x==x |"'-' '!=' ')' ...
R[125]= PrimaryExp = '(' ConstExp ')' ;"| syntaxState162
syntaxState163 x==x |"'identifier' 'intConstant' 'uintConstant' ...
R[15]= RandomTokens = null ;"| syntaxState163
syntaxState165 x==x |"'¥' 
R[8]= MicroDefinition = '#define' 'identifier' '(' ')' RandomTokens ;"| syntaxState165
```
